# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
When objects that are at the point of tipping, any forces that are not
When tipping one of the normal contact forces dissapears, all on one of the contacts ^y5UMVSlW

A uniform plank AB of length 2m and weight 20N rests on two supports, one 40cm from A and the other 60cm from B
a) Find the reaction force at each support
b) A cat of mass 40N starts from the centre of the plank and walks towards A. How far from A is the cat when the plank tips? ^hGmq7nsP

At point of tilting, R  = 0 ^eZ2W2XES

Q ^7FHEab1N
